1b2(1): 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag nyid gsang ba chen po rdo rje 'dzin

2a1(1): myur du 'dul bar byed pa/ bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi snying po de kho na nyid las phyung ba/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gtso bo sa chen
2a2(1): po mthar phyin pa la rab tu zhugs pa/ 'dod pa'i khams dang gzugs kyi khams su gtogs pa'i dbang phyug lha'i rigs rnams kyi bdag po chen po lcang lo can gyi gnas dang ri
2a3(1): rab kyi gnas kyi gnod sbyin rnams kyi ded dpon chen po de/ 'og min gyi gnas lha'i rgyal po'i khang bzangs na bzhugs te/ dus gsum du rnam par bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas
2a4(1): rnams kyi sku gsung thugs kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i 'od zer sna tshogs bkye nas tshig 'di skad du bskul te/ kye kye gsang bdag rdo rje 'dzin// khyod ni sangs rgyas thams cad
2b1(1): kyis// bstan pa dam pa bsrung ba yi// mthu stobs bdag por dbang bskur te// dam tshig chen po de gzigs la// sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba las// 'jigs byed 'jigs par byed pa yi// sku mchog drag
2b2(1): po'i gsung dang bcas// gtum po'i thugs kyi shugs phyung la// gdul dka' ma lus 'dul ba'i phyir// sprul pa snga 'phrul phrin las kyis// sngon gyi thugs dam rol par mdzod// ces pa bskul ma thag tu bcom
2b3(1): ldan 'das de sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad pa'i dus la bab par mkhyen nas/ nyid kyi sku gsung thugs zhi ba chos nyid de bzhin las ma g.yos kyang gdul bar bya ba'i yul drag shul can rnams la gzigs
2b4(1): nas/ phyogs bcu nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sku'i rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa khro bo chen po'i gzugs 'di lta ste/ sku mdog mthing nag zhal
2b5(1): dgu pa la/ g.yas kyi zhal ni kham nag gtsigs pa/ g.yon gyi zhal ni smug nag bsdus pa/ dbus kyi zhal ni mthing nag khro zhing rngam pa/ phyag g.yas kyi rdo rje 'bar bas g.yon gyi thod khrag dkrug cing gsol ba/
2b6(1): g.yas 'og ma brgyad na lha chen po bsgral ba'i mgo gcad de bsnams la/ g.yon gyi 'og ma brgyad na klu chen po brgyad kyi mgo bsnams pa/ de dag kyang g.yang gzhi dang bcas pa/ g.yas kyi spyan
3a1(1): dgu gyen la bzlog pa/ g.yon gyi spyan dgu 'phreng la gzigs pa/ dbus kyi spyan dgu thur la sdang mig mdzad pa/ khro gnyer drag po dpral bar bsdus pa/ shangs nas srid pa'i rlung drag po 'tshub
3a2(1): pa/ zhal nas bskal pa'i me 'bar ba/ mche ba dmar po bar snang khams su gtsigs pa/ sma ra ag tshom sprin bzhin du gtib pa// dbu skra ral pa kham nag srid pa'i rtse mor 'bar zhing 'khyil ba/ snyan nas
3a3(1): gdug pa'i sgra chen po 'byin pa/ sbrul gyi chun pos yan lag dkris pa/ bdud dang rA tra bsgral ba dang glang po che'i pags pa na bzar gsol ba/ stag gi lpags pas sku smad dkris pa/ khrag dang zhag gi thig le
3a4(1): dang ri mos brgyan pa// thal chen gyis lus la byugs pa/ thod pa skam po dang rlon pa dang / sha khrag ra ri can gyis phreng bar byas nas brgyan pa/ zhabs brgyad kyis tshangs pa dang khyab 'jug dang dbang phyug chen

3b5(1): g.yog gi tshogs dang bcas pa dag gis/ rang rang gi gnas nas myur ba dngang zhing skrag la 'jigs pa dang yang ba'i sems dang / dul ba'i sems kyis 'thon te/ bcom ldan 'das de'i spyan sngar rlung drag
3b6(1): po'i shugs kyis rab tu bskyod pa'i shing bal gyi 'dab ma bzhin du rang dbang med par lhags par gyur te/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa dang / khyad par du mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams na
4a1(1): gling bzhi dang / rgya mtsho chen po dang / rol pa'i chu klu'i gnas dang bcas pa/ ri rab chen po dang / ri bdun gyi gnod sbyin gyi tshogs dang / lha'i gnas 'dod pa'i khams dang / gzugs kyi khams
4a2(1): dang / gzugs med pa'i khams dang bcas pa dang / dmyal ba dang / yi dwags dang / byol song gi skye gnas na gnas pa dang / 'dzam bu'i gling gi sa'i cha na gnas pa'i dregs pa can rnams so so nas rang rang
4a3(1): gi mdun na drag po chen po'i sku gzi byin dpag tu med pa/ gzhan dag gis nye ba'i thugs mi thub pa re re 'dug pa mthong ste/ de dag thams cad tha dad du rang rang gi sde dpon chen po rnams la skyabs su 'gro
4a4(1): bar byed do// sde dpon chen po rnams ni 'jigs byed chen po'i sku gsang ba pa'i bdag po de la rang gi 'khor dang bcas te skyabs su 'gro bar byed de/ thams cad kyi rang rang gi gzugs dang longs spyod dang

4a6(1): ma du phrag dzaH/ dun+ti ma du dzaH/ zhes 'jig rten gyi dbang phyug chen po yab yum bdud pho mo dang bcas pa rnams kyis rang rang gi ming phul ba'o// de nas gshin rje'i ded dpon rang gi tshogs dang bcas pas rang
4b1(1): rang gi ming dang srog dang bcas pa phul ba// hrIHSh+TaM kr-iSh+Ta ya ma pre ta dzaH/ ma ma ya mun+ti b+hi tri dzaHzhes phul lo// de nas srin po'i sde dpon rang gi 'khor dang bcas pa'i ming gi snying po// rak+Sha ra sha ra ma ti rak+Sha ma

9a1(1): gzugs brnyan gsal btab ste// rang gi ming gi snying po dang / gcod 'phrog yi ge spos te bzlas// dus tshad grangs dang mtshan ma yis// tshad bzung ma nor grub pa yis// rtags la phab ste las
9a2(1): la sbyar// nga nyid rjes su sgrub byed pas// dregs pa myur du dbang du sdud// zhes bka' stsal to// 'jig rten pa'i ded dpon gyi tshogs nye bar sgrub pa'i rtsa ba'i las kyi gnyer gtad pa'i le'u ste gnyis
9a3(1): pa'o// // de nas rab tu bshad bya ba// 'di dag kun la ngas bshad pa'i// sde dpon chen po rang gnas nas// bod dang gzhug dang mnyes pa dang // bstod dang thugs dam bskul ba dang // tshig
9a4(1): brjod 'di yis bstan par bya// thugs rje rnam dag dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor nas// chos sku stong nyid dbyings las ma g.yos kyang // 'jig rten dregs pa'i tshogs rnams 'dul ba'i phyir// khro chen dpa' gtum
9a5(1): 'jigs byed skur bstan pa// thugs dam dgyes bskul gsang ba'i yum dang bcas// ma rtogs shugs kyis 'dul phyir gshegs su gsol// dregs pa'i dbang phyug 'jig rten lha yi gtso// 'dod pa'i lha mo
9a6(1): bde chen 'byung gnas ma// 'khor tshogs drag shul mthu stobs dpung gi bdag/ khro gtum gdug pa'i rtsal 'chang dpal dang ldan// rdo rje 'chang gi bka' bzhin rjes su sgrub// dam tshig rjes dgongs gnas
9b1(1): 'dir gshegs su gsol// badz+ra sarba duSh+Tan+ta a tan ya e dza b+h+yo/ a gats+tsha sa ma ya hring hring / dur khrod gsang ba mchog gi dkyil 'khor 'dir// lha chen nyi zla pad+ma'i gdan steng du// bcom ldan khro rgyal rngam
9b2(1): brjid 'bar ba'i sku// yab yum dgyes par rol cing bzhugs su gsol// snang srid dregs pa ma lus ded dpon gtso// 'dod khams bdag po dgyes mdzad yum dang bcas// lha srin tshogs kyi gtso chen
9b3(1): 'khor dang bcas// phrin las mthun pa'i gdan la bzhugs su gsol// badz+ra sarba duSh+TAn a ta na ya e dza b+h+yo// sa ma ya sti ta badz+ra hUM dzaHdus gsum sangs rgyas thugs kyi snying po mchog/ chos kyi sku las
9b4(1): gzugs sku 'gro don sprul// tshe btsan 'gran zla med pa khro bo'i rje// dbang sdud yum dang bcas la phyag 'tshal bstod// phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba ma lus sras dang bcas// dam bcas bstan pa'i tshul bsrung 'jig
9b5(1): rten mgon// zhing bcu sgrol mdzad phrin las drag shul can// sde dpon sum cu'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo// badz+ra sarba duSh+TAn a ta na ya e dza b+h+yo// na ma A ra li / dpal chen dregs pa kun 'dul yab yum
9b6(1): la// sku gsung thugs mnyes mchod pa 'bul ba ni// gdugs dang rgyal mtshan ba dan bla re dang // phreng ba phye ma lnga ldi za ra tshags// bdug spos me tog mar me chab bsil dang // gzugs mdzes sgra snyan dri/
10a1(1): zhim ro bro dang // reg 'jam 'dod yon ma lus ji snyed pa'i// 'phags pa'i thun mong mchod tshogs bzhes su gsol// khyad par gsang ba'i mchod pa 'bul ba ni// dus gsum gnas su sbyangs
10a2(1): pa'i sha rus khrag/ dug lnga sman du grub pa'i dam tshig rdzas// stobs mchog nus pa ba ling mchod pa dngos// thugs rjes mthun pa'i ngang gis bzhes su gsol// dpal chen yab yum bka' bzhin rjes sgrub
10a3(1): pa'i// dbang phyug chen po yab yum mnga' bdag rje// 'jig rten 'das kyang 'khor ba'i cha lugs 'dzin// bka' yi bstan srung sde dpon sum cu la// 'dod pa'i yon tan mchod cing sbyin pa ni// dkar dmar
10a4(1): ser ldang la sogs mdog/ zlum po gru bzhi la sogs dbyibs// che chung sbom phra ring thung tshad// mdzes dang mi mdzes sdug mi sdug/ 'byung ba rten 'brel rol mo'i sgra// glu tshig bstod dbyangs snyan pa'i
10a5(1): tshig/ spos sman bdud rtsi me tog dri// bsreg sungs baM sungs dri dang ngad// kha mngar tsha skyur bska ba dang / lan tshwa sbod dang bye sgyu dang // 'jam rtsub bsil yang tsha dang bro// so so'i yon tan tshogs dang
10a6(1): bcas// 'dod dgu 'bul gyis bzhes su gsol// bdud rtsi lnga dang sha lnga dang // don snying lnga dang 'byung ba lnga// dbang po lnga dang yul lnga dang // phung po lnga dang nang grol lnga// 'tshe zhing gsod dang bar du
10b1(1): gcod// gdug par sems shing log par lta// mi mthun phyogs lngar bcas pa rnams// so sor 'bul gyis bzhes su gsol// badz+ra sarba duSh+Tan a ta na ya e tsa dza b+h+yo/ ma hA ba lin+ta/ a mr-i ta/ su ka ta/ mAM sa//
10b2(1): rak+ta/ bi ba ta/ bA su ta/ la ma ta/ i daM gr-ih+Nan+ta sa ma du/ kha kha/ khA hi khA hi/ bcom ldan dpal chen dregs pa kun 'dul dang // yum chen khams gsum spyi 'dul 'khor bcas kyi// sku mdog 'gyur med me
10b3(1): long gzugs brnyan bzhin// gsal zhing rtog med snang ba ma 'gags pa// sku lnga lhun grub rdzogs pa'i dngos grub gsol// gsung mchog 'gag med brag cha sgra brnyan bzhin// snyan dang mi snyan grag stong tshangs
10b4(1): pa'i gsung // gsung dbyangs nam mkha'i mthas khyab dngos grub gsol// thugs mchog spros bral bsam 'das chos kyi dbyings// mi rtog bde chen thabs dang shes rab dang / rtsol med mi g.yo mchog gi
10b5(1): dngos grub gsol// yon tan brjod kyis mi lang sna tshogs yod// 'das dang ma 'das mchog dang thun mong gi/ grub pa brgyad dang mthar zug dngos grub gsol// 'jigs pa brgyad sogs zhi dang 'byor pa
10b6(1): rgyas// log lha mos pa'i tshul gyis dbang du sdud// mngon spyod dgra bgegs 'dul ba'i dngos grub gsol// badz+ra sarba duSh+Tan a ta na ya e dza kA ya sid+d+hi/ bAka sid+d+hi/ tsit+ta sid+d+hi/ gu Na sid+d+hi/ kar+m+ma sid+d+hi/ hUM hUM hUM/
11a1(1): bcom ldan dpal chen dregs pa kun 'dul ni// dbu dgu phyag ni bco brgyad de// sku mdog mthing nag khro zhing rngam// g.yas kyi zhal gsum spug nag bgrad// g.yon gyi zhal gsum kham nag
11a2(1): gtsigs// dbu skra ral pa me dpung 'bar// spyan dgu sdang mig bzlog cing bgrad// shangs nas srid pa'i rlung nag 'thor// snyan nas stong gsum 'brug sgra 'dir// sma ra ag tshom me ltar 'bar// mche
11a3(1): gtsigs srid gsum rtsa ba gcod// phyag dgu g.yas g.yon dang po yis// rdo rje thod khrag dkrug cing gsol// g.yas kyi phyag brgyad 'og ma na// dregs pa'i lha brgyad bsgral ba yi// g.yang gzhi mgo bor
11a4(1): bcas te bsnams// g.yon gyi phyag brgyad 'og ma na// klu chen brgyad kyi b+han d+ha ru// dregs pa'i snying khrag bkang nas gsol// dpa' bo'i chas brgyad sku la rdzogs// zhabs brgyad brkyang bskum dor stabs
11a5(1): // khams gsum bdag po sde bzhi mnan// yum chen khams gsum spyi 'dul ma// zhal gcig phyag gnyis mthing nag sku// rdo rje 'phyar zhing thod khrag stobs// gnyis med thugs kyi phrin las kyis// 'jig
11a6(1): rten dregs pa bran du 'khol// lha srin sde brgyad las la 'gyed// dgra bgegs gdug pa rtsad nas gcod// khro rgyal gtso la phyag 'tshal bstod// dpal gyi bka' bzhin las mdzad pa'i// lha chen dbang phyug
11b1(1): chen po ni// zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog mthing / phyag g.yas gri gug tsit+ta g.yon// lha mo u ma de ba ni// sku mdog mthing nag gtso la 'dud// phyag g.yas rtse gsum thod khrag g.yon// seng ge glang chen
11b2(1): gdan la bzhugs// sde dpon dregs pa kun gyi gtso// yab yum sku la phyag 'tshal bstod// bdud kyi rgyal po'i sde dpon ni// khram shing g.yas la dgra sta g.yon// bdud rta nag po'i khri la bzhugs// sbyor yum
11b3(1): bdud mo re ma ti// khram bam g.yas la nad rkyal g.yon// bong bu ga dmar gdan la bzhugs// gshin rje'i sde dpon chen po ni// be con g.yas la thod dbyug g.yon// sbyor yum gshin rje za byed mo// phyag
11b4(1): gnyis srid pa'i 'khor lo bskor// yab yum ma he chu glang gnon// srin po'i sde dpon glog phreng can// phyag gnyis thog ser 'dril zhing 'phen// srin mo sbal mgo khrag mig ma// phyag g.yas phur pa khrag phor
11b5(1): g.yon// yab yum 'brug dang rnga mo gnon// gnod sbyin sde dpon me dpal ni// phyag g.yas rin chen g.yon ral gri// sbyor yum gnod sbyin nag mo ni// phyag g.yas spu gri g.yon sbyang mo// stag seng phag mo
11b6(1): zhabs kyis mnan// gza' bdud ded dpon chen po ni// phyag g.yas mda' gzhu g.yon sbrul zhags// sku smad sbrul 'khril 'brug chen gnon// sbyor yum thog gi bu yug can// g.yas g.yon phyag gis thog
12a1(1): @/ ser 'bebs// klu rgyal ded dpon chen po ni// phyag g.yas sbrul zhags g.yon nad rkyal// sbyor yum klu mo nag mo ni// sbrul mgo phyag mtshan yab kyi tshul// yab yum chu srin rus sbal
12a2(1): gnon// phyogs bzhi steng 'og gnas bzhugs pa'i// dregs pa'i ded dpon 'di dag ni// kun kyang sku mdog mthing nag la// khros pa'i cha byad 'jigs tshul can// dur khrod g.yang gzhi'i chas kyis
12a3(1): brgyan// rang gi tshogs 'dus 'phrin las mdzad// yab yum bcas la phyag 'tshal bstod// gnod sbyin lha yi rgyal po ni// shel gri ba dan dkar po 'dzin// rgod dkar ru bzangs zhabs kyis mnan// gnam
12a4(1): rgyal chen po ded dpon ni// phyag g.yas ldan dkar g.yon shel gri// rta dkar rdog dmar zhabs kyis mnan// spyi bdud rgyal po gu rum rtse// phyag g.yas ba dan g.yon shel gri// zhabs gnyis rdo rta gro bo
12a5(1): gnon// dkar po'i ded dpon chen po gsum// shar phyogs gnas la phyag 'tshal bstod// srid pa'i ma mo ded dpon mo// 'khor lo g.yas la me long g.yon// zhabs gnyis 'brug mo mgo dgu
12a6(1): gnon// sngags kyi srung ma chen mo ni// tsit+ta g.yas la sbrang mo g.yon// dre rta nag mo zhabs kyis gnon// mkha' 'gro nag mo mgyogs byed ma// rgyu zhags g.yas la mtshon grug g.yon// so bya nag mo zhabs
12b1(1): kyis gnon// nag mo'i ded dpon ma mo gsum// lho phyogs gnas la phyag 'tshal bstod// rdo rje bdud 'dul nag po ni// g.yas g.yon phyag gis thun khrag 'phen// brag btsan srog zan dmar po ni// mda'
12b2(1): gzhu 'phen zhing dar dmar 'phyar// che btsan 'gong rgyal chen po ni// shang lang dang ni zhags pa 'dzin// dmar po'i ded dpon rgyal po gsum// kun kyang rta dmar zhags kyis gnon// nub phyogs skyong la
12b3(1): phyag 'tshal bstod// bi nA ta ka bgegs kyi rgyal// phyag g.yas kha T+wAM g.yon thod khrag/ phyi rol skyong ba'i mu stegs gtso// tri shUl g.yas la thod khrag g.yon// dmu bdud chen po phrag med ni// mda' gzhu dang
12b4(1): ni shang lang 'dzin// nag po'i tshogs kyi ded dpon gsum// bdud rta nag po zhabs kyis gnon// byang phyogs gnas la phyag 'tshal bstod// tshangs pa'i rgyal po srog gi bdag/ spu gri g.yas la nyi zhags
12b5(1): g.yon// seng ge dkar po zhabs kyis gnon// bdud kyi rgyal po nor gyi bdag/ bdud zhags g.yas la spu gri g.yon// ban glang sna rings zhabs kyis gnon// sku lha'i rgyal po yul gyi bdag/ phyag g.yas rdo
12b6(1): rje g.yon ba dan// ra dkar gnam ru zhabs kyis gnon// nag po chen po tshogs kyi bdag/ phyag g.yas be con g.yon thod khrag/ rta nag mgyogs pa zhabs kyis gnon// phyogs kyi sde dpon chen po bzhi// sku
13a1(1): mdog dkar ser dmar nag mdzes// sgo bzhir gnas la phyag 'tshal bstod// sde dpon dregs pa 'di dag ni// khro zhing gtum pa'i tshul 'chang zhing // na bza' g.yang gzhi 'jigs pa'i
13a2(1): chas// sna tshogs mdzes pa'i rgyan dang ldan// rang gi 'khor g.yog tshogs kyis bskor// sprul pa'i cho 'phrul bsam mi khyab// mchod bstod chen pos khyed bsgrubs na// so so'i tshogs 'dul phrin las
13a3(1): mdzod// zhes brjod ting 'dzin ldan pa yis// dregs pa'i ded dpon mchod cing bstod// 'di ltar spyod pa'i rnal 'byor gyis// 'jig rten gtso bdag gzhung bzhin bsgrub// rdo rje 'dzin dang gnyis su
13a4(1): med// zhes bka' stsal to// 'jig rten gyi ded dpon nye bar bsgrub pa rdo rje'i dam tshig mchod bstod kyi le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas rab tu bshad bya ba// 'jig rten dregs pa dbang sdud
13a5(1): cing // tshar gcad las la skol ba'i phyir// byin brlabs gnas pa'i dbang bskur bshad// gsang zhing dben pa'i gnas dag tu// sngar bshad las kyi pho brang bsham// yo byad rdzas kyi khyad par 'phags// ma
13a6(1): lus par ni gzung bar bya// rdo rje 'chang ba rjes 'brang bcas// mtshan nyid ldan pa mngon sum sbyar// dus kyi grangs dang mtshan ma'i rtags// bsnyen pa'i lung bzhin brtson par 'bad// gzugs brnyan bdag
13b1(1): po slob ma rnams// khyad par gnas pa'i sta gon bya// bris dang rkos pa la sogs pa'i// sde dpon rnams kyi gzugs brnyan dang // phur pa grangs dang mnyam par dgram// gzhan yang bum pa mchod gtor
13b2(1): dang // dug gtor thun gtor thun rdzas dang // sha khrag bshos chang bza' btung sogs// rgyal mtshan ba dan mda' dang gzhu// dpa' ba'i chas dang rol mo'i sgra/ rab tu brdar zhing mdzes par bsham// rdo rje
13b3(1): 'dzin pas ting 'dzin gsal// las kyi rgya pos mchod bstod bya// rgyu dang mdangs kyis thugs dam bskang // bshags dral bcugs sbyang dbab pa bya// mos shing spros bdag dang ba yis// bdud 'dul gtso la
13b4(1): skyabs su 'gro// bstan pa bsrung bar sems bskyed de// bla ma sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin// he ru ka dang gnyis med la// gdug byed log lta 'dul nus pa'i// mthu dbang chen po'i gzhung 'tshal gyis// brtse
13b5(1): ba'i thugs kyis dgongs nas ni/ dkyil 'khor dam par gzhug tu gsol// nyon cig skal ldan rigs kyi bu// dus gsum sangs rgyas sku gsung thugs// gnas pa'i bstan pa bsrung ba'i phyir// spro bas 'jug
13b6(1): pa khyod lags kyis// mngon spyod brtul zhugs dam pa yis// dam tshig chen po'i sar 'dug shog/ mgon po he ru ka dpal rje// 'dul ba'i 'khor tshogs bcas pa yi// drag shul spyod pa'i pho brang du// mdzes
14a1(1): pa'i me tog bdag dbul gyis// rdo rje dam tshig 'di bzhes la// dregs pa 'dul nus dngos grub gsol// pra ti gr-ih+Na puSh+pa hUM/ dpal ldan rdo rje 'chang ba yi// rjes 'jug rigs kyi bu khyod
14a2(1): ni// thog ma med nas da lta'i bar// bstan pa bsrung ba'i skal ldan te// sde dpon dbang chen dkyil 'khor 'dir// bstan la rab dga'i sems kyis ltos// badz+ra ya sa ma ya ma d+ha la tsag shu bra be sha ya phaT/ rdo
14a3(1): rje bdud rtsi dam tshig chu// 'di las dus gsum 'da' mi bya// grub pa'i 'bras bu gnyis yin te// tshul bzhin mi 'da' bros dor cig/ ma hA sa ma ya i dan+te nA ra kAn ShA ba mi laM/ rdo rje 'dzin pa bka' drin/
14a4(1): che// thugs rjes rtag tu byin brlab phyir// 'di nas rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi bar// mthu stobs dngos grub stsal du gsol// badz+ra sa ma ya tsit+ta sid+d+hi sid+d+hi hUM/ thog ma'i sangs rgyas sras bcas kyi// rjes su bsgrub
14a5(1): pa bdag yin gyis// 'jig rten 'das dang ma 'das pa'i// lha dang dregs pa mthu stobs can// gtso dang 'khor du bcas rnams kyis// sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig dgongs// rdo rje slob ma rig 'dzin
14a6(1): la// dbang bskur dngos grub rtsol mdzad pa// nus chen rtags mtshan bstan du gsol// rdo rje 'dzin pa dpal ldan gyis// khri stan chen po'i steng 'dug la/ snod ldan slob ma mdun bzhag ste// dkyil 'khor
14b1(1): gnas pa'i bum pa yis// sku gsung thugs su dbang bskur bya/ gnyen po gtso dang gdul bya'i yul// dregs chen yab yum 'khor bcas kyi// mdzes pa'i sku gzugs sku yi dbang // so so'i tshig bstod snying po
14b2(1): dang // smon lam bcas pa gsung gi'o// rang rgyud gnas dag don rtags kyis// chos skur dbang bskur thugs kyi'o// rigs sbyangs stobs la ngang gis gsal// phur pa drag shul rdzas kyis dbang // mchod
14b3(1): gtor bshos cha sku gsung thugs// ma lus mnyes par byed pas te// yo byad tshogs kyi longs spyod spel// rgyal mtshan ba dan sgra dang bcas// dus rnams kun du mnga' thang rgyas// sha khrag dug gtor thun rdzas
14b4(1): rnams// dregs pa'i ded dpon dbang sdud cing // pho nya phrin las bskul mdzad de// mngon spyod gdug pa tshar gcad dbang // 'di dag kyang ni gzugs brnyan sgra// don ngo shes pas dbang bskur te// chos
14b5(1): kun spyi dang dregs pa yi// sde dpon so so'i dam tshig rtsal// thugs rje dang ni rtogs pa yis// rang bzhin don gyis sgrol byed pa'i// dpag med don chen 'dir 'dus te// tha dad mi gnas cig yin
14b6(1): gzung dang 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid kyis// phyi nang 'khor bcas so sor snang // ma lus dbang bsdu zil mnan phyir// so so'i snying po tshad kyis bstim// nga rgyal brtan po mdun du skyes// don snying sha rus
15a1(1): khrag sogs bza'// dug gsum tshar gcad dbyings nas dbyung // gzugs brnyan bstims la rab tu gsal// dbang bsdu las bcol 'dul ba'i phyir// zhabs 'og mnan te bran bzhin
15a2(1): bsgo// dam tshig rdzas mchod sngar bzhin gso// dam tshig dpag cing bstod skul bcol// 'jig rten lha srin khyed rnams kyang // nga dang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// zhal mthong lung bstan mchog stsal
15a3(1): ba// srid pa'i sa bon phra mo yis// da rung 'jig rten las la spyod// rang rgyud rtsub mos phan gnod sbyor// da ni dka' yi dam tshig bzung // ma 'ongs dus na bsgrub bya dang // sgrub par byed pa de dag
15a4(1): dang // mnyam par kun la dbang sgyur te// chos nyid rig pa'i rgyal po rdzogs// theg mchog ma 'dres cir yang ston// ma lus myur du rdzogs bya'i phyir// rgyab tshab spyir bor bzhag gnas pa// kun tu bzang po

15a6(1): ba// dregs pa'i 'khor tshogs mnyes bya'i phyir// mthun rdzas gzugs kyis bskang ba ni// ri bo'i rtse bo'i chu bo'i mdo// 'jig rten dbang phyug 'du gnas su// skal med yul la mchod sbyin gnas// thod
15b1(1): mkhar re'u mig dgu sogs sam// yang na gling bzhi ri rab brtsig/ 'bru dang sha khrag sna tshogs pa// rin chen spos sman me tog stsal// dregs pa bdag po so so yi// gzugs brnyan rang gi 'khor dang
15b2(1): bcas// sku mdog phyag mtshan yongs rdzogs shing // rang gi gdan khri bzhon par bcibs// ri rab thod mkhar yang stengs su// lha chen yab yum 'khor bcas bzhugs// bang rim re'u mig dang po
15b3(1): gsum// bdud dang gshin rje srin po dang // gnod sbyin gza' dang klu rnams kyi// sde dpon yab yum 'khor bcas dgod// gnyis po la ni dkar po dang / nag po dmar po nag po'o// sde dpon bcu gnyis
15b4(1): gnas su bya// gsum pa'i phyogs bzhir sgo srung bzhi// 'khor bcas rang gi gnas su dgod// tha ma gsum mam bzhi pa la// phyi nang gsang ba sbas pa la// gsang ba'i gter dang drag po sngags// las byed/
15b5(1): btags chags lha ma srin// sde brgyad gzugs brnyan gnas su dgod// gtso chen sum cu'i mthun rdzas ni// rang gi gdan nam bzhon pa yi// srog chags gzugs ni lnga'am bcu// brgya 'am stong ngam grub tshad
15b6(1): bya// skyes pa bud med glang chen rta// ban glang ra lug bya ra khyi// longs spyod skong rdzas sngar bzhin no// sde brgyad phal pa kun la ni// shes ldan mi dang byol song ste// 'dab chags gcan gzan ri dwags dang //
16a1(1): 'dab chags gcan gzan ri dwags dang // sa chur gnas dang dud 'gro tshogs// mthong zos dran pa rnams kyi gzugs// ji ltar nus pa'i grangs kyis bskor// 'di dag bskang ba'i yo byad
16a2(1): ni// 'gro ba'i glud du 'bul ba ni// rin chen ngar mi rgyan ldan dang // nam mkha' sems kyi gzugs brnyan dang // sku gsung thugs ldan rgyang bu dang // shing glud yul mkhar mtshon pa dang // skyes pa bud med
16a3(1): byad dang // rgyal mtshan ba dan ru mtshon rnams// dregs pa so so'i sku mdog dang // mthun pa grangs mnyam gnas su dgod// mchod gtor bshis cha mar me dang / gling tshad chung ngu de bzhin no// bzlog bsad
16a4(1): drag po zor gyi rdzas// sbyin pa'i sa la zor phor du// gru gsum mnyam byas dug khrag dang / thun rdzas sna tshogs stsal ba dang // gdug pa'i shig gi rtsang phur dang // b+han d+ha dug thun gtor mar bcas// bzhi

24a1(1): 'dus pa'i tshogs// dbang po'i yul gyi longs spyod dang // gtsang sbra'i rtog pa sbyang ba'i rdzas// 'dod chags bzhi dang 'bru bcud rtsi// gnyis med pha rol snang byed pa// rang gi ngang du mnyes byed
24a2(1): cing // so so'i mtshan dang dpe byad dag/ nges par bstan pa nang gi'o// sems dang sems la bstar ba'i tshogs// thams cad ye nas dkyil 'khor che// ma bcos rang bzhin lhun gyis grub// lung nas ma lus
24a3(1): 'dus pa las// chos gzhan med de yul nyid dang // yul du 'dzin pa snang ba'i bdag/ gnyis med rtogs shing khong du chud// mchod bstod rab tu gsang ba yi// lus las sprul zhing bsgrubs pas sku// 'bru
24a4(1): bcu sgra yi 'khor lo gsung / rang grol snying po ma bcos thugs// lha klu gnod sbyin btsan dang bdud// srin po gza' dang mo rigs rnams// dregs shing gdug pa khro zhing gtum// myur mgyogs rmugs shing
24a5(1): 'thibs pa dang // dregs dang dbyings pa so so'i sde// ri rab bshos gtsang rgyan dang bcas// 'bru lug snying rtse tsa ru'i dbyibs// dkar dmar bcud ldan dmigs kyis mchod// pha dang rgyal po grogs dag
24a6(1): lha// ma dang rje khol bran lta bu// brten pa rang gi tshul yin no// che btsan dbang gi dngos grub dang // longs spyod 'phel zhing mngag par blang // rgyud 'jam skyabs che bka' nyan zhing // drag rtsal ldan zhing slar
24b1(1): mi ldog/ shin tu nye ba yon tan te// rang la rtsub cing 'tshe ba dang // longs spyod mi 'byor mi 'phrod dang // glo bur nad kyis gzir byed cing // slar ldog bkra shis nyams pa dang // bsgo ba mi nyan don med
24b2(1): cing // rang rgyud rtsub cing khengs pa dang // rigs rgyud ma smin kun gyis brnyas// bsam don mi grub mnga' thang nyams// rgyud don sbas pa ma shes skyon// khrims kyi bdag po lta bu'i lha// gnad kyis bcing zhing
24b3(1): bsgrub par bya// dbang chen pha dang mtshungs pa'i bdud// mtshungs med grogs dang 'dra ba'i btsan// gnod sbyin khrims kyi gtso lta bu// srin po srog la rgol ba'i gshed// gza' rgod lag yan gzhon lta
24b4(1): bu// sdong bu dug sbrul lta bu'i klu// mo rgyud dbang chen rje dpon ma// mtshungs ldan de yi gnyen por bsgrub// khugs su ma bcug bsgo mi nyan// se long gnad med bdud du 'gyur// bcud phur ma thebs slar la
24b5(1): ldog/ rang gi rab rol ma bzhar g.yel// lto ba ma dkrugs las mi myur// log non ma ldan bdag nyid stob// dbang du ma 'dus bsgo mi nyan// gnad kyi man ngag brgyad kyis ni// mchod bstod bsgrub ste phrin

25a1(1): rnams// drag po'i las la sbyar ba ni// dur khrod gdug pa'i gnas dag tu// rtsa ba'i bsnyen pa sngon song nas// so so'i mthun pa'i rdzas bsar te// drag po'i las kyi khang pa ni// e dbyibs sum
25a2(1): cu ldan par bsham// phyi nang gsang ba sku gsung thugs// gnas byin brlab dang bskang dang mchod// spyi dang so sor bsngags pa dag/ rab tu bde bar 'dod pas dmigs// gzugs sgra bsam pa'i nus pa
25a3(1): yis// lus dang lus kyi 'phrul 'khor dang / srog dang srog gi gnyen po yis// sems dang sems kyi ngo bo las// phyi nang kun tu bsngags pa ste// 'phro 'du 'od kyis drang zhing dgug/ rang gzhan dmigs pa de
25a4(1): la stim// sha lus khrag sogs ma lus bzas// dregs pa'i sde dpon sku gsung thugs// ma lus mnyes pa 'di yis bya// gang la dmigs pa tshad kyis sgrol// ting nge 'dzin gyi brtul zhugs kyis// bul dang myur
25a5(1): ba blo yi stobs// 'di la the tshom mi bya ste// rdo rje 'chang chen gsang ba'i bka'// gal te 'bar bas mngon spyod cing // myur du 'pho bar bya ba ni// rno dpal tsha rtsub dri nga ba'i// yam shing gdug pas dbyibs

25b1(1): dbul// gtso dang 'khor gyi rab phye ba'i// drag po'i tshig gis rab tu bgrang // dregs pa'i bdag po so so yi// che brjod gnad dang bcas pa yis// stab cing sbyin pa rim bzhin bya// drang srong phrin las rdzogs
25b2(1): par bskul// thal chen dang ni drag po'i rdzas// rme khrag gsum dang gsod byed gsum// mtshon bral rin chen gsum gyi dbyig/ rang byung bkra shis bzlog pa'i rdzas// nang du 'du 'phror sbyar ba ni// sgra tshig ting
25b3(1): nge 'dzin ldan pas// stobs chen 'khor los dbab cing 'phang // dregs pa 'khor bcas las su dmigs// gzhan yang mchod rdzas gzugs brnyan byas// rab tu bstan pa'i dmigs pas bstim// 'gyu gnas
